Domestic News Roundup 80

He Jingwu, Director of the Pinghan Railway Bureau, and Qian Zongze, Director of the Longhai Railway Bureau, have both concurrently served as Transportation Commanders for their respective railways. With the end of military operations, preparations are underway to transfer all military transport matters on both railways back to the management of the railway bureaus. However, the Longhai Railway Bureau and the Zhengzhou Pinghan Railway Workers' Union report that railway employees and workers have been in arrears with their salaries for half a year, resulting in extremely difficult living conditions. Employees of the Longhai Railway Bureau fear that excessive accumulation of salary arrears will make it difficult to recover them, and have established a Salary Arrears Liquidation Committee to demand compensation from the railway bureau. In addition, the Pinghan Railway Workers' Union, due to the inability of workers to maintain their livelihoods, recently submitted a document to He Yingqin, head of the Zhengzhou Military Headquarters, requesting assistance. It is reported that He has forwarded the original document to the railway bureau for proper handling. (October 31st)

<Cao Fulin Supervises Troops Heading East>

Monitoring Sun and Gao's Troops for Demobilization and Reorganization

Qingdao Communication: Military affairs in Shandong have long concluded. Although there are still a few bandit gangs sporadically looting in various counties of eastern Shandong, the local garrisons are sufficient to suppress them, and there seems to be no need to mobilize large forces. However, the other day, Shandong Provincial Chairman Han Fuqu suddenly ordered Cao Fulin, commander of the 14th Army, to lead troops eastward to pacify the bandit troubles in Jiaodong. He also ordered the 22nd Division, 29th Division, 73rd Division, and 74th Division to be under Cao's command and dispatch, and they departed overnight as if facing a major enemy. Feeling that the matter was sudden, I took a train to Jiaoxian yesterday (3rd) to visit Commander Cao and inquire about the reason for this dispatch of troops. The details of my interview are recorded below:

Troop Deployment: Cao's troops are heading east in two routes. The 73rd Division, commanded by Zhan Shutang, disembarked at Gaomi and proceeded to the Zhucheng area. The 22nd Division, commanded by Gu Liangmin, and the directly subordinate units of the 14th Army disembarked at Jiaoxian and proceeded to Rizhao and other places. Earlier, a unit of Zhan's division stationed in Jiaoxian was ordered to depart from Jiaoxian to Gaomi on the night of the 1st, and followed the army. At 6:00 AM on the 2nd, a train full of soldiers from the 65th Brigade of the 22nd Division arrived in Jiaoxian. After a short rest, they were led southward by Brigade Commander Tang Yaoxun. At 10:00 AM, another train arrived, led by Commander Cao, carrying directly subordinate units, including a cavalry battalion, an artillery battalion, and a pistol battalion. After Cao disembarked, he took a car into the city and temporarily resided in the 14th Army headquarters. The cavalry and artillery battalions immediately proceeded forward. The pistol battalion remained in Jiaoxian to maintain defense. The "Taishan" armored train followed behind and was expected to arrive in Jiaoxian around the night of the 3rd.

Resolving Gao's Troops: At 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the 3rd, I visited Commander Cao, but Cao was out. Wang Yabo, a staff officer from the army headquarters, received me in his place. I asked what the mission of the army's eastward deployment was. Wang said that the army came because there were unsettling rumors about the remnants of Gao Jianbai's troops stationed in Rizhao. Chairman Han specifically ordered the army to go and resolve Gao's troops. Tang's brigade has already advanced southward from Jiaonan to the Haizhou area, and the 26th Army, commanded by Chen Yaohan, has been ordered to intercept them to prevent them from fleeing south. They have now received a telegram from Gao's troops expressing their willingness to obey the provincial government's orders for demobilization and reorganization. This matter is expected to be resolved peacefully. I also asked if Commander Cao was going south. Wang replied that Commander Cao plans to temporarily reside in Jiaocheng and has telegraphed Chairman Han about the handling of the situation. Whether he goes south will be determined after receiving the Chairman's telegram. I also asked if the personnel from the Eight Grand Bureaus had come as well. Wang replied that personnel from various bureaus had brought a part of the assistance, including Chief of Staff Wang Shiqi, Chief of the Staff Department Su Erchang, Adjutant Cao Jinming, and Military Law Director Li Xiuren. Wang solemnly declared that there were many misunderstandings outside regarding this dispatch, which they did not understand. During this period of military conclusion, if bloodshed can be avoided, it will be a blessing for the people. If various miscellaneous troops can repent and surrender, Chairman Han will never blame the past to show leniency.

Readjusting Sun's Troops: It is heard that this time Cao's eastward deployment is not only to resolve Gao's troops but also to supervise Sun Silang's troops stationed in Zhucheng. Sun's troops were originally reorganized from the Jiaoxian bandit army led by Ji Xiaoxi. After Ji was executed, the troops were commanded by Sun, numbering about a thousand people, and stationed in Zhucheng. Recently, Chairman Han ordered Sun's troops to proceed to Jinan to await demobilization and reorganization, but Sun delayed in complying. Therefore, Chairman Han ordered Cao to lead troops to supervise their departure. Now, Zhan's division has successively arrived in Zhucheng territory. Knowing that resistance is impossible, Sun's troops have expressed their willingness to go to Jinan to await demobilization and reorganization. It is also reported that a unit has already arrived at the Gaomi station to wait for trains to go west, and the rest are successively departing. It is heard that Commander Cao will transfer the divisions back to their original defenses after Gao and Sun's troops have actually undergone demobilization and reorganization, and return to the province to report on his mission (October 4th).

Hunanese Urge the Completion of the Yuehan Railway

Raising Civil Shares in Guangdong, Hunan, and Hubei Provinces

To Be Returned to the Central Government After Fifteen Years

Changsha Communication: The Yuehan Railway spans over two thousand li and is crucial to the commerce of Hunan, Guangdong, and Hubei provinces. Among them, the Zhushao section (from Zhuzhou in Hunan to Shaoguan in Guangdong), measuring eight hundred and ninety li, remains unfinished. Furthermore, over eight million yuan in principal and interest of civil shares (i.e., rice and salt public shares) owed to the Hunan section have not been repaid. Four-fifths of the Zhushao section lies in Hunan, so the Hunanese are the most affected and the most eager to complete it. As the Fourth Plenary Session is scheduled to open on the 12th of this month, the Hunan Rehabilitation Committee has specifically requested the prompt completion of the Yuehan Railway to develop production in the southeast. At the same time, the Hunan branch of the Yuehan Railway Promotion Association has also formulated a plan to complete this road. The plan proposes that the people of Hunan, Hubei, and Guangdong provinces temporarily raise shares to build it, and after fifteen years, the government will prepare funds to recover it for direct management, so that the principle of railway nationalization is not contradicted, and the road can be completed early with the help of the people. The method of raising funds jointly borne by the three provinces has been drafted and submitted to the Fourth Plenary Session for adoption and implementation yesterday. At the same time, telegrams were sent to the Guangdong and Hubei branches of the Yuehan Railway Promotion Association, requesting consistent support. The proposed methods for completing the railway through civil shares and for raising funds are recorded below:

(A) Temporary Methods for Completing with Civil Shares: (1) Designate the people of Hunan, Guangdong, and Hubei provinces to raise shares. The Central Government will send one or two experts in engineering to supervise the project and its materials. According to the unfinished line, only Hunan and Guangdong provinces are responsible. According to the benefits of completion, all three provinces will benefit. Hunan already has nearly 10 million yuan of rice and salt public shares as a base. Merchants in Guangdong and Hubei are wealthy. Raising over 30 million yuan will be as easy as turning one's hand. (2) Set a deadline of four or five years for completion. (3) Stipulate that fifteen years after the completion and opening of traffic, the road will be returned to the central government for direct management (returning it at the shortest possible time limit). This can avoid capitalists from monopolizing it from the middle, which does not hinder the capital restriction program. Moreover, after fifteen years, the central government will obtain this road without labor, which is not only indistinguishable from nationalization but even better than nationalization. (4) Quickly return the rice and salt public shares to Hunan Province to serve as a fund for the Hunan section. (5) Please allocate a few tenths of reliable central funds to supplement the insufficient strength of the people as government capital.

(B) Methods for Raising Funds in the Three Provinces: (1) The total cost of the entire line, the Zhushao section, which is 445 kilometers long, equivalent to 890 Chinese li, regarding engineering materials, construction, and other expenses, is set at 45 million yuan. Calculated on the basis of completion in five years, 9 million yuan is needed each year. (2) The approximate amount allocated to the three provinces is calculated annually. Guangdong will bear 2 million yuan, totaling 10 million yuan in the above numbers. Hubei will bear 2 million yuan, totaling 9 million yuan in the above numbers. (Note: The Guangdong section is shorter than the Hunan section, but the allocated amount is greater than Hunan's because Guangdong is a wealthier area and fulfillment is easier. Moreover, the commerce of Hubei merchants will receive equal benefits once this road is open, so they cannot but have the obligation to take shares.) (3) Hunan's fundraising methods: I. Under the port tax, Taiwan, Sichuan, Huai, and Guangdong salt taxes are calculated to yield about 400,000 yuan annually. (Note: This donation originated at the end of the Qing Dynasty. The prescribed use was to build the Yuehan Railway. Later, the road was not built and the donation was not stopped. All the annual income was transferred to the central government for other uses. The central government should approve the recovery of the original port tax. Moreover, the salt tax surcharge is no less than 400,000 yuan per month, all of which goes to the central government. It should be appropriate to slightly transfer it.) II. Under the public shares, the principal of the long-owed rice and salt public shares should have been returned long ago. Last year, the Yuehan Railway Promotion Association submitted a request to the provincial government to forward it to the Ministry of Railways and the Ministry of Communications for repayment to replenish the Hunan road fund. It was once approved for repayment. Later, after investigation, the number of public shares actually received and owed was only over 8 million yuan. Although the government is unable to repay the full amount, repaying 200,000 yuan per month from the national treasury should be within the possible range. A total of 2.4 million yuan can be obtained annually, and the full amount can be repaid in three years. III. Under the additional items, an additional 2.7 million yuan can be collected annually from land tax, likin, and miscellaneous taxes. (Note: This fund was originally designated for the construction of the highway. Now that the road bureau has been reorganized and incorporated into the province, this fund has been discontinued. It is proposed to extend it for two years and transfer it to Yuehan Railway shares, but the extension is stipulated from the start of construction to the fourth year, when the rice and salt public shares have been fully repaid.) IV. Under the designated items, the provincial government will designate 50,000 yuan per month, totaling 600,000 yuan annually. (Note: If Hunan's taxation is seriously rectified and the long-standing malpractices are eliminated, an additional 500,000 to 600,000 yuan can be collected annually, which is also expected. Designating this number is also negligible.) V. Under the fundraising items, Hunan's commercial circles, such as the Changsha, Hongjiang, Changde, Jinshi, Hengzhou, Xiangtan, and Yiyang chambers of commerce, and mining merchants and Huai merchants, can raise 500,000 yuan annually if they entrust road shares. The completion of this road will not only avoid the losses from the Communist bandits' donations, but also the development of commerce will surely yield several times the benefits. They will enthusiastically transport and strive to be the first. Calculating the above items only on the Hunan side, over 4 million yuan can be obtained annually in the first two or three years, and over 3.67 million yuan can be obtained annually in the fourth and fifth years, which is more than a million yuan or six or seven hundred thousand yuan more than the original quota. Listing this number is to prevent insufficient coverage, in order to use it as a supplement. Guangdong is a wealthy area and Hankou is a commercial center. Raising the number of shares allocated annually is easier and requires no other consideration. Therefore, the above is omitted. In short, no matter where the funds are collected from, stocks will be issued uniformly. How to give interest each year, how to distribute dividends per share, and how to end the central government's recovery at a price after fifteen years will be planned after the company is established, and regulations will be formulated for compliance (November 4th).

The Andong Customs House is Destroyed by Ronin 81

The Reason Originated from Investigating Tax Evasion

Customs Officer Mr. Yang is Severely Injured

Andong Communication: Andong port has the reputation of being a hub for tax evasion, known throughout the world. Adjacent to the border of Korea, separated only by the Yalu River, tax evasion is extremely convenient and difficult for customs to investigate. There are also so-called "affiliated territories" that are beyond the reach of Chinese administrative police power. Japanese ronin take advantage of this special region to secretly organize tax evasion groups, employing thousands of Korean coolies to specialize in smuggling goods in and out of Andong and Sinuiju. Every night, countless small boats smuggle fabrics and silks from Sinuiju to Andong, numbering around a hundred small boats. According to customs officers' investigations, countless small boats full of piece goods are seen departing from Sinuiju in the evening, and by the next morning, they have all disappeared without a trace. The boats transport the empty goods after the night when the customs patrol ships return to port and land on the seven islands in the affiliated territory in Andong, then transport them to the inland for sale. Customs Superintendent of Andong Pilasolak determined that the customs losses were too great, and not only transferred additional inspectors from other ports to Andong for severe inspection this year but also recruited more than a dozen customs inspectors to help patrol. The Japanese tax evasion group then slightly curbed its activities. However, these ronin not only did not repent but harbored resentment. In July of this year, they threw customs officer He into the Yalu River to vent their anger. Fortunately, Mr. He was well-versed in swimming, so even though he drifted for forty minutes, he was able to escape. Recently, because the market price of gold bars differs greatly from the exchange rate, the group smuggled gold bars out of the country to profit from the difference. However, because the opportunity was not hidden, the customs seized several cases a month ago, totaling more than 1,300 taels. These ronin then resented the customs to the bone and instigated the Japanese police station in the affiliated territory to interfere, arresting the customs officer in the police station on the false charge of carrying weapons and violating the treaty. The Japanese Consul then came out to protest, prohibiting customs personnel from exercising their duties in the affiliated territory. Unexpectedly, the Customs Superintendent Pilasolak not only did not show weakness and submit but declared that he would transfer this case to the central government for resolution through diplomatic means. Thus, their plan failed again. Unexpectedly, the Japanese ronin became even more ferocious. A few days ago, when the customs seized gold bars, a sudden mob of hundreds of people completely destroyed the windows, glass, and furniture of the Chinese customs house. The Japanese police station stood by and watched. The other day, when the customs seized another batch of gold bars and were inspecting them, a sudden mob of hundreds of people came with steel knives, sticks, bricks, and stones, indiscriminately beating any customs officers they saw. Some customs officers escaped, some had swollen heads and broken skin, and Mr. Yang Shuqi was brutally cut off his right hand by a thug. At that time, blood flowed like a fountain and he fainted on the ground. Seeing that they had caused a disaster, the mob scattered in a riot. Mr. Yang is now in the hospital in critical condition and it is difficult to predict whether he will survive. At the time, several Japanese policemen were on the scene and deliberately avoided going when they saw the thugs approaching. After seeing that the man had been killed (because Yang fell to the ground and they all said he was dead), they came out to disperse the mob and capture the murderers. However, the local Japanese newspaper does not acknowledge that the murderer has been caught. They are afraid that if Yang dies, they will have to go through the motions of handling a few years of imprisonment under the law. It is better to insist that the murderer is at large, so they don't have to go through the motions at all (November 2nd).

Opening of the Zhejiang Provincial Agriculture and Mining Conference 82

The first Agriculture and Mining Conference held by the Zhejiang Provincial Government's Agriculture and Mining Department opened at 9:00 AM on the 6th. Attendees included representatives from 21 counties with convenient transportation and nearby affiliated agencies. Important officials from the department were also present, totaling more than 50 people. Zhang Jingjiang, Chairman of the Provincial Government, and Cheng Zhenjun, Director of the Construction Department, also attended the meeting. First, Director Huo Baoshu delivered the opening remarks, stating in essence that China is not actually poor, but is mired in poverty because industry is not developing. Today, this conference is specifically opened to discuss the implementation of industrial plans in order to seek cooperation and achieve early results. Then, Director Cheng delivered a speech on behalf of Chairman Zhang, followed by simple reports from various affiliated agencies. In the afternoon, group discussions were held, with 27 proposals divided into special affairs, agriculture, forestry, water conservancy, fisheries, and cooperation groups. It is reported that a plenary session will be held again this morning (7th) to discuss everything.

Suzhou 83

Unreasonable Trouble by Wounded Soldiers: There are approximately several hundred wounded soldiers receiving treatment at the 17th Rear Hospital in Huqiu, Suzhou. Yesterday (7th) morning, wounded soldiers in the hospital, dissatisfied with the quality of the meals and vegetables, used this as an excuse to cause trouble for Director Xu, demanding improved treatment, resulting in an uncontrollable conflict. Director Xu telegraphed Jiang Xiaoxian, commander of the 4th Garrison Regiment in Fengqiao, Suzhou, requesting that a team be dispatched immediately to suppress them. Commander Jiang immediately dispatched military police. Unexpectedly, the wounded soldiers continued to cause trouble unreasonably. The military police opened fire with more than ten rifles, and the wounded soldiers finally calmed down. At 4:00 PM, the military police arrested 16 wounded soldiers who were the ringleaders of the disturbance and escorted them back to the regimental headquarters for disposition.

Execution by Strangulation of a Parricide: Wang Jinbao, a resident of Jiading, 32 years old, was sentenced to death for killing a member of his senior family and killing an unknown soldier. Zhang Bingxiang, Wang Huisheng, and other cases were concluded after three trials, sentencing them to death. After the application for retrial, the verdict was still death. After being reviewed by the Procuratorate of the Supreme Court, it was submitted to the Ministry of Justice for approval and execution. The other day (6th), the High Court received an order from the Procuratorate of the Supreme Court, approving the strangulation of Wang Jinbao. Yesterday (7th) morning at 9:00 AM, after receiving the order, the High Procuratorate dispatched Prosecutor Jin Henian to supervise the police to the Third Branch Prison in Siqian Street to retrieve Wang Jinbao, verify his identity, and escort him to the execution ground for strangulation.

Wuxi 84

A Robber Who Snatched Jewelry is Arrested on the Spot: A female worker named Chen Xiaomei worked at a silk factory outside the South Gate. The other day (afternoon), Xiaomei finished work at the factory and was going home when she suddenly encountered a robber named Dai Awun stopping her on the road at Caobu Bridge, snatching a gold ring from Xiaomei's hand. At that time, Xiaomei immediately shouted for help and was slapped several times by the robber, causing her face and other places to be bruised, swollen, and bleeding. Afterwards, Xiaomei reported to Wang, the head of the Third Public Security Bureau in charge. After receiving the report, Wang immediately dispatched armed police officers to pursue and arrest the robber Dai Awun and bring him to the bureau. Head Wang opened the court for a preliminary hearing. The suspect Dai provided cunning words and firmly denied the robbery. Yesterday, a document was prepared and submitted to the Branch Security Bureau for interrogation.

An Investigation is Requested for Fraudulent Acquisition of Wealth: The locals Long Yunzhang and Huang Cangyu had a deep friendship and both worked in the National Road Construction Association, distributing books and newspapers in Fujian, Guangdong, and other places. All accounts were handled by Huang Cangyu. This summer, Long Yunzhang suddenly fell ill and immediately handed over 400 yuan of promotional book fees under his personal name to Huang Cangyu for transfer to the Shanghai General Association's Book Department under Long Yunzhang's name. Unexpectedly, Huang was ill-intentioned and remitted all the money under his own name. It wasn't until August that the General Association asked Long for the money that Long realized he had been deceived. He then pursued Huang Cangyu for the previous money, but Huang did not admit that he had previously owed the money. Long Yunzhang was weak and helpless after being repeatedly deceived. Yesterday, he submitted a report to the county government requesting investigation.

A Shocking Incident of Robbery, Kidnapping, and Extortion: The fifteenth district (Qingcheng City), Lianrong Town, North Qifang area is densely populated with shops, and transportation is very convenient. There is a slightly resident Hua Jinhan, who previously served as a city director of Qingcheng City and a prefect of Taizhou. He has a wealth of property, owning four to five thousand mu of good land. His residence is a five-bay facade house facing north, and he also has a huge house under the Liulong Bridge in the city. Hua is now eighty-one years old and has a wife and a concubine. His wife died long ago, and his concubine Xue is fifty years old. His wife bore two sons and two daughters. The eldest son, Zhongfan, is forty years old and currently runs a Yuanfengsheng grocery store in Beiqifang, which is doing well. The second son, Rongsheng, is thirty years old and previously served as a secretary in Zhu Zhijun's Public Security Bureau. Both brothers are married. Hua's eldest daughter, Xiangying, also known as Miss San, is over thirty years old and has not yet married. Rongsheng often lives in the main house under Liulong Bridge in the city. However, Hua Jinhan has been suffering from dementia for many years and is unable to move. The silver and money in the house are all managed by his daughter Xiangying. Unexpectedly, around ten o'clock on the night before last (6th), twenty to thirty bandits speaking the Jiangyin dialect suddenly came. They were wearing long and short clothes, resembling rural people, and each was holding a pistol, box cannon, knife, stick, electric flashlight, and other weapons. After arriving in the town, they dispersed guards to prevent pedestrians from passing through and cut the telephone lines connecting the town, cutting off communications. The rest of the bandits went to Lian in the east and struck Hua Jinhan's house hard door. At that time, there was a thief stealing the cabbage planted by Hua's family. The bandits immediately grabbed him and forbade him to speak out. Since Hua's door was closed, the bandits used a bamboo pole to climb over the wall from outside and enter the courtyard and immediately fired a few shots to show off their power. At that time, Hua Jinhan had already been awakened from his dream and was in a state of panic. Xiangying and the fourth lady immediately fled to a neighboring house of the same clan to hide in the attic. After entering, the bandits immediately went through the rooms and searched everywhere and chased them to Jinhan to tell the location of the hidden ocean. They were robbed of 200 yuan in cash, and the clothes and jewelry in the boxes and kitchens were all robbed, totaling a loss of thousands of yuan.

Page 10

In addition, Tandan's deeds (which are mortgaged to the Hua family) and bank-books were all robbed. Unexpectedly, the bandits were still not satisfied after being full, so they tied up Hua's concubine Xue. At the same time, they found that Hua Xiangying's sisters were hiding next door, so they immediately went to look for them and used an electric flashlight to light them up. See Xiangying and drag her upside down and tie her away. When the bandits were leaving, they said to the principal Hua Jinhan: Prepare 20,000 yuan in cash and come and pick it up. When you contact us, we will have a letter to notify you within these three days. After speaking, they opened the door and went out to fire shots as a demonstration, shouting and going to Zhangcun浜 on the border of Wuxi and Cheng, and escorted Hua Xue and Hua Xiangying into the bandit ship and drove towards Jiangyin. It was also heard that the bandits originally planned to bind Hua Jinhan, but after asking Hua's concubine Xue to beg for help, she was willing to replace her husband with herself, so the bandits tied up Xue and Xiangying and left.

The Liyang Old String Embezzlement Case will be Transferred to the Court for Investigation: The Liyang County Bureau's Old String Embezzlement Case involves members of the party department and local bullies. There are already eleven people who have been arrested and sent to the province. The Standing Committee of the Provincial Party Rectification Committee discussed the arrest of Shi Taorong, Shi Qinglian, and Hu Jinghua, who are in custody in Liyang County. After the arrest, it was proposed that the three men were suspected of major offenses in the case. After discussion, it was decided to suspend the party department's position. Although Shi and others submitted two documents, they have been trying to defend the case, but the documents have not been approved. On the afternoon of the 6th, Qian Jiaxiang, section chief of the Provincial Government's Third Section, went to the Provincial Public Security Bureau with a staff member to interrogate Shi Taorong and others. Shi and others cited past participation in the revolutionary work, and asked the provincial government to investigate the matter in detail and punish the embezzlement personnel to prove that they did not pay bribes. After an hour of research, there were no results. Wang Pingling, the whistleblower in this case, arrived in the town a few days ago, and representatives of the Liyang Township Association in Beijing, Xie Pengnian, Zhang Dasan, and Huang Huaizhen, went to the provincial government to petition, requesting that the case be thoroughly investigated and severely punished to purify the palace, and listed the eleven people who were arrested and in custody in three categories: (1) Pan Bin, Shen Zhiqing, and Huang Xingan are suspected of embezzlement; (2) Zheng Chengyuan, Cao Qingzhi, Di Zhen, Shi Taorong, Shi Qinglian, and Hu Jinghua are suspected of bribery; and (3) Ren Shuchun and Zhou Shi are suspected of knowing the situation, and requested that the above persons be transferred to the judiciary for thorough investigation and strict interrogation to clarify the truth.

Changshu 86

Case of Robbery and Kidnapping in Xiyang Town 87

In Xiyang Town, Fushan District of this county, which borders the Yangtze River, bandits appear and disappear unpredictably. The locals have become accustomed to it and are not at all vigilant. Unexpectedly, around 12 o'clock the night before (the 5th), more than twenty pirates landed from the riverbank and swarmed into the home of traditional Chinese medicine doctor Zhang Chengqi, demanding silver dollars. Zhang replied that he had no money, and if they insisted, he requested that they set a date and address so he could have time to raise the funds and pay them the full amount. The pirates refused and immediately began looting, obtaining only a little over twenty silver dollars and some clothing.

The pirates, still unsatisfied, then kidnapped Zhang. Upon exiting the Zhang residence, they saw the house of Zhang Baoqi, a farmer on the opposite bank, which looked quite good, and mistakenly assumed it was a wealthy household. They went around to the other side of the river, broke down the door, and ransacked the place, only to find a few dozen copper coins. Thereupon, they kidnapped the sixty-four-year-old farmer Zhang Baoqi and his six-year-old son as well.

Next, they went to the home of Qian Yongkang in town, who ran a cotton business. He had recently returned from Donglai Town in the Nansha District with over nine hundred silver dollars worth of goods, which were all stolen. Afterward, they went to the home of a Qiu surname, stealing over two thousand silver dollars in total.

Seeing that there were no more homes to rob, the bandits took their hostages and returned to the riverbank. They encountered three sentries from the port's customs patrol boat. The pirates rushed forward and bound the sentries. The sentries begged and pleaded before they were released, but their firearms and ammunition were all taken. Then, the pirates boarded their boat and headed north.

After the incident, according to townspeople, before the pirates arrived in town, they had sent several men to pry open the public telephone to prevent the news from leaking. Furthermore, the fishermen guarding the crab weirs said that when the pirates came, Zheng Yushan, a migrant from Wangshi Town, held an electric torch and led the way.

Currently, the victims have reported the matter to the Fushan District Office and have also telegraphed the county government requesting a rescue of the hostages.

Central Government Interpretation of Industry and Commerce Associations 96

The Provincial Consolidation and Training Department of Industry and Commerce Associations inquired with the central government about the standard for initiators of industry and commerce associations and industrial associations. The directive received states that the revised organizational plan for people's organizations has the following: the third section on organizational procedures for people's organizations states, "Unless otherwise stipulated by law, the organization follows the following procedure." This organizational procedure regarding the need for joint signature from fifty or more initiators is only applicable to organizations that do not have separate legal regulations. As the initiators of industry and commerce associations and industrial associations are already separately stipulated in the specific laws of each organization, the provisions of those specific laws should be followed. After receiving the order, the Provincial Training Department has instructed the counties to comply.

Robbery Case in Lujia Lane 99

Yangzhou 100

Public Trial of the Yanghuo Road Incident 101

The case of the forced labor road construction from Yangzhou to Huojia Bridge on March 13th, in which workers rioted and assaulted officials of the Construction Bureau due to demands for food, has reached August. The Public Security Bureau and police teams have successively apprehended Xia Guohuai, Xie Zhengfu, Xia Shaotang, Shi Youfa, Wang Changsen, and other five individuals involved in the case and handed them over to the court for handling. As the case has been investigated and prosecuted by the prosecutor's office, it was brought to court and publicly tried yesterday (the 5th).

Those present included the victims, former Director of the Construction Bureau Wang Daoping, technicians Zhou Chun, Xu Xiyi, and Dong Shushen, as well as the five arrested defendants, the defense lawyers Hu Zhen and Dai Tianqiu, and other witnesses. People of this county attached great importance to this case, so there were more than a hundred spectators in attendance. The case was presided over by President Chen of the court, with prosecutor Lu, who investigated the case, invited to the court.

First, the prosecutor stood up and announced the reasons for the public prosecution of Xia Guohuai and the other four, charging them with violating criminal law. Then, President Chen separately and sequentially examined the case for three hours. The prosecutor then rose and said that the case had been debated to conclusion and requested the presiding judge to pronounce judgment. Wang Changsen was declared not guilty, and Xia Guohuai and the other four were found guilty of obstructing official duties and various crimes of injury and damage. At that time, the defense lawyers Hu and Dai stood up and said that the investigation procedures in this case could not be considered complete, and the penalties for Xia Guohuai and the other four may not be appropriate. They requested that the court wait for the county government to send a detailed investigation report to the court, and then the court could determine the truth before making a judgment. As a result, the defendants were all returned to custody to await a scheduled pronouncement.

Xiaoshan 106

Court Investigates Tobacco Case Fines Thoroughly 107

Li Guanbao and Shen Damao, detectives of the Xiaoshan County Public Security Bureau, previously cracked down on Zhou Da's tobacco den in Qianqing. The tobacco offender Zhou Da was sent to the county court, and after interrogation, the judge sentenced Zhou to a fine of one hundred yuan, with fifty yuan to be distributed among the officers as a reward. This amount was not issued, and someone filed a complaint with the High Court. The High Court ordered the Xiaoshan County Government to investigate and respond. According to the Xiaoshan County Court Prosecutor's Office, the money had been issued to the Public Security Bureau.

Yesterday, the Zhejiang High Court, in order to understand the facts, dispatched Chief Prosecutor Zhang to Xiaoshan to investigate the case in person and summoned detectives Li Guanbao and Shen Damao to court. They confirmed that they had not received the reward money, and it is still unknown who pocketed it.

Director of Consolidated Tax Bureau Transferred 108

It is heard in Xiaoshan that Dai Yiqun, Director of the Consolidated Tax Bureau, has been transferred to serve as Director of the Ningbo Consolidated Tax Bureau according to provincial orders. Chu Xingzai, Director of the Pinghu Consolidated Tax Bureau, has been appointed to fill the Xiaoshan vacancy. Chu arrived in Xiaoshan on the 6th to take over.

Education News 109

Important News 110

Two Declarations from Students of National Central University 111

Explaining the Truth of the Turmoil and the Standards for Selecting a President "Disturbing Situation" 112

The undercurrents between the National Central University Student Union and the National Central University Student Association: The students of National Central University held a meeting the other day to make suggestions regarding the presidential issue and to prevent all activities of the current National Central University Student Union, forming a special committee to handle all the resolutions of the general assembly, which was deemed legal. However, the National Central University Student Union believes that the number of people present at the fourth and subsequent resolutions of the general assembly was insufficient, making the resolutions illegal, causing a dispute between the two sides. Separate declarations were also made externally. The National Central University Student Union also sent representatives to the Municipal Party Headquarters yesterday (the 7th) to request the cessation of the activities of the presidium of the National Central University Student Association general assembly, Liu Shichao, Tang Ziquan, and Tu Juyou. The declarations of both sides are recorded below.

Declaration of the First Student General Assembly 113

(1) The Course of the Current Turmoil 114

Since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing and this university was reorganized, three years have passed. During these three years, the name of this university has changed several times, the funding of this university has been shaken several times, and the administrative system of this university has been reorganized several times due to the revision of the University Organization Law. To this day, it has not left the initial stage. During this period, all administrative matters have not been on track, and the results obtained are far from expectations. The students of this university deeply know that an ideal university cannot be achieved in two or three years. This phenomenon is inevitable in the initial stages of general universities in the country. However, feeling the ardent expectations of society and the importance of our own mission, we have always been deeply vigilant. For three years, the students of this university have sought to strengthen the foundation of the university externally and have prepared for the progress of the university internally. This is also the initial intention of this movement to improve university affairs.

Several weeks ago, students Tu Juyou and others initiated a movement to improve university affairs with the backing of more than six hundred students. Although the issues involved were very numerous, and there were criticisms against one or two staff members, it was nothing more than a manifestation of their love for the university and their desire to work hard and make progress, which could represent the psychology of all students. Even the means they took did not exceed the permissible scope. The students of this university believed that this legitimate request would be accepted by the university. Therefore, after making the request, they waited quietly for the university's reply and did not expand the turmoil. However, Xu Zicheng and others suddenly responded to Tu and others' proposal by soliciting student signatures. The next day, when Xu and others submitted the proposal to the president, they added additional clauses, and some matters involved individuals. Therefore, students who had signed Xu and others' proposal declared that it was inconsistent with their original intention of signing, and the unanimous opinion among the students suddenly became divergent. The next day, President Zhang resigned and went to Shanghai, merging the original three academic affairs offices into the General Affairs Office, appointing Huang Pu as the Director of General Affairs. The entire student body and faculty of this university believed that changing the administrative organization of the university without formal approval from the academic affairs meeting was inappropriate, and this incongruous General Affairs Office fundamentally conflicted with the University Organization Law, so they insisted on opposing it. Huang disregarded the situation and rashly took office on October 27th. During Huang's report at the memorial week ceremony, students questioned him, and Huang could not answer, so he announced that he would no longer be responsible for National Central University. This is the general course of the current turmoil.

(2) Our Current Attitude 115

Although this university has been spared from disintegration in this precarious situation, the government has no solution for the time being, and opportunists are trying to take advantage of it. Therefore, leaflets under false pretenses are often found on campus, and malicious attacks with ulterior motives are rising outside the university, confusing right and wrong. Recognizing the urgency of the situation, the entire student body of this university had to give it a clear and correct correction. Therefore, on November 5th, a general assembly was held, and the following points were unanimously resolved as a solemn expression: (1) Before the presidential issue is resolved, although the university affairs are temporarily maintained by the joint agreement of the deans, the students should also organize a special committee to be responsible for handling all resolutions of the general assembly. All groups that have not been formally recognized by the general assembly, such as the previous committee to protect the university movement and the committee to rescue the university and eliminate traitors, should be denied the right to express opinions to the outside world in order to maintain the dignity of the university and prevent exploitation by villains. (2) All the students of our university deeply know the mission they bear and are now focusing on attending classes. The presidential issue can only be resolved by waiting for the reasonable solution from our government. After several discussions, we also feel that it is necessary to propose the following standards for the successor: First, someone who is respected by the public for their academic and moral standing and has no bureaucratic habits; second, someone who can focus on their duties and has the determination and ability to develop National Central University; (3) someone who has achieved success in running higher education; (4) someone with a considerable history in the Party and the country. The entire student body of our university believes that the above provisions are the minimum standards that a university president should have. We will make every effort to achieve them with determination. Any successor who meets these standards, we will vow to support with all our strength. Any president who does not meet these standards, we will vow to oppose with all our strength. The entire student body of our university has no personal preferences, but we have the greatest determination for the development of the university's future.

(3) Hopes for Social Figures and the Government 116

This university is now in a critical situation. The entire student body deeply knows that social figures and government authorities are criticizing us because of their excessive expectations for this university. Rumors are spreading, some believe that the university's academic atmosphere is corrupt and its ideology is mixed, and some even believe that it is a battleground for nationalists and communists. The entire student body now wants to declare to society that our university has not dared to lag behind in implementing the Three Principles of the People education in recent years. All students know their responsibilities are heavy and are aware of self-encouragement. Since the turmoil at our university began a month ago, all students and faculty have attended classes as usual, waiting for a legal solution from the government, and there are no such facts as rumored by the outside world. We firmly believe that if the government authorities have a long-term vision, they will fully adopt the standards for the selection of a president that we have proposed in order to promote academics and make a prompt and wise decision. National Central University is located in the capital and is observed by China and foreign countries. The entire student body vows to work hard for the development of its future with twelve points of determination and perseverance and hopes that social figures and government authorities will provide deep support for this determination and perseverance. This declaration is hereby made.

Declaration of the Student Union 117

Executing Legal Proposals in the Resolutions of the General Assembly 118

Denying Illegal Proposals After the Quorum of the General Assembly Was Lacking 119

Unfortunately, since disputes arose over university affairs, the school has been full of crises and dangerous situations. The newspapers have been noisy, and the public has been panicked. However, our students have remained calm in the face of chaos with a genuine love for the school, so the sounds of music have not been interrupted, and villains have not been able to succeed. Since President Zhang telegraphed his firm resignation, the school has been in a state of panic due to the lack of anyone responsible. In view of this, the student union has repeatedly asked the government to resolve the presidential issue as soon as possible to avoid neglecting studies. The general assembly on the 5th of the month was also intended to concentrate the will of all students to jointly seek the safety of the school. More than eight hundred people attended the assembly, which was a legally constituted formal assembly. The assembly passed (1) not expressing an attitude on President Zhang's resignation; (2) four criteria for the new president: (A) Someone who is respected by the public for their academic and moral standing and has no bureaucratic habits; (B) someone who can focus on their duties and has the determination and ability to develop National Central University; (C) someone who has achieved success in running higher education; (D) someone with a considerable history in the Party and the country. During the discussion of the fourth proposal, attendees withdrew one after another, because the nature of the proposal was insinuating and seemed to have another purpose, and the few speakers were strong-willed and eloquent, with ulterior motives. Subsequently, students successively discovered the "quorum" issue (only about two hundred people at this time). In accordance with Section 23 of Sun Yat-sen's Preliminary Principles of Democracy, the chairman (Liu Shichao) was asked to stop the discussion and declare the meeting adjourned. However, Liu Shichao was not familiar with the Preliminary Principles of Democracy and intended to manipulate the meeting, so he ignored the request and continued the discussion. Therefore, those who accused the chairman of being昏庸 continued to withdraw one after another. Afterward, there were only fifty or sixty people in attendance. In order to promote Sun Yat-sen's teachings, the union should deny the illegal proposals (from the fourth proposal onwards) after the general assembly found a lack of quorum. On the one hand, we request the Party Headquarters to stop Liu Shichao and others from implementing the unworkable and unfounded proposals from the fourth proposal onwards in order to demonstrate justice. As for the proposals before the third proposal, they have been resolved by the public opinion of our majority of students. The union sincerely accepts and has executed them to comfort the expectations of our students and lay the foundation for the new life of the school. There is also something that must be declared: The union did not hold a re-election because the representative council secretary, Ti Dong, did not follow the charter. The union repeatedly urged the secretariat, but the secretariat made excuses and delayed again and again. The intentions are obvious, and the responsibility lies there. The union is entrusted by all students and only knows how to act according to the will of all students. Success or failure, profit or loss, we do not know the work. If it benefits all students or is the will of all students, we will not hesitate to go through fire and water. Conversely, anything that harms the students or is not the will of the majority of students will be treated with hatred. Wherever justice lies, reason has no regrets.

Respectfully announced, hoping for your clear understanding. November 8th.

Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office Describes the Education Funding Situation 120

To the Jiangsu Education Funding Committee 121

The Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office sent a letter to the Jiangsu Education Funding Committee, stating that the office had previously received a letter from principals of provincial middle and primary schools, including Zhang Tong, severely questioning the arrears in various expenses. It has sent a detailed reply clarifying the methods of raising and distributing funds for July and August and the extreme difficulties of the education funding situation, and requested the prompt dispatch of an accountant to audit the office. These exchanges of official letters have been published in the education columns of various newspapers on November 3rd. It is assumed that everyone has read them and is aware of the outline. Recently, the Joint Association of Faculty and Staff of Provincial Schools issued a serious declaration with phrases such as "Education funds are by no means exhausted" and "Who are you trying to deceive with false claims of shortages?"

The source of education special funds is limited to the slaughter tax and tooth tax and busy canal special funds. There are no newly opened tax sources, but expenditures have been expanding year by year. The budget lists a subsidy of 500,000 from the Ministry of Finance and the Department of Finance. On the surface, it appears that revenue and expenditure are in balance, but in reality, there are inevitable situations of虚收实支. It is already insufficient to cover expenses. In addition, due to natural disasters and banditry in previous years, tax revenues have sharply decreased, making it impossible to cope with the situation. The detailed situation has been disclosed in the reply to the Education Department and does not need to be repeated.

As for the claim that the salaries of the office staff are paid every half month, it is not known that payment requires a notification form to be audited by the Audit Committee. If payments are made twice a month, it is inconsistent with the methods of various schools. How could the Audit Committee approve such absurd claims? This is not worth a knowing person's smile. However, it is said that there are layers of obscurity in the office, and the economy has not been made public. If we remain silent, outsiders who do not know the content may inevitably be doubtful. Therefore, it is necessary to defend ourselves. Since the independence of education funds in March of the 14th year, there has been concern that there may be abuses in the income. Therefore, the Education Gold Treasury of the China Communications Jiangsu Three Banks was established. All counties remit funds directly to the Education Gold Treasury, which issues formal and deputy treasury receipts. The treasury receipt is stored by the fund-remitting agency. The formal treasury receipt is sent to the Management Office for inspection, clarification, and registration. The Management Office never directly receives cash. No agency directly delivers cash to the Management Office. This is how the income is handled.

Again, fearing that the expenditure is not verified, the Audit Committee was organized. The committee meets twice a month to audit the accounts. All payments are made only after a notification form is filled out, reviewed, approved, and stamped by the Audit Committee, and then stamped by the Education Department and the Director of the Management Office. The fund-receiving agency then goes to the Gold Treasury to collect the funds. They cannot make payments on their own, and they cannot withdraw funds independently. This is how the expenditure is handled.

From this, it can be seen that the power of income is controlled by the Education Gold Treasury, and the power of expenditure is controlled by the Audit Committee. The Management Office is only in a management position. Where do the obscurities come from? Even in the case of the slaughter tax, which is most competitive, the Management Office adheres to its principles, firmly adheres to the established regulations, and treats all committee-recognized merchants with equal standards, regardless of the amount offered, and requires all to pay 20% deposit in advance. There is no room for flexibility and no obscurities. Furthermore, at the end of each month, the income and expenditure are compiled into a report and printed and sent to all schools and agencies for public inspection. How is it that these faculty and staff have never seen it? Why do they say that the economy has not been made public? This is truly incomprehensible.

Currently, the funds for July and August are being raised, either by borrowing busy canal funds from various counties or by borrowing cash from banks. The slaughter tax deposit should be refunded when the merchants' recognition period expires. Reluctantly, all funds are being transferred and used as資. It is already竭泽而渔. Even so, the principals and faculty of various schools still suspect that the funds will not be issued and falsely accuse us of obscurities. We should ask the esteemed committee to borrow from the Education Department for verification of the previous letter and promptly send an accountant to the office to audit the accounts to dispel suspicions and clarify the truth. However, various schools need funds every month, and the treasury is empty. The busy canal tax has not yet been征. In this difficult time, we are at a loss. The esteemed committee is responsible for the overall planning of education funds for the entire province. At this critical juncture, when bankruptcy is imminent, please promptly convene a meeting to discuss rescue methods and agree on opening up new taxes so that the office can follow and the various schools can rely on to maintain themselves. We await your orders with great anticipation.

There is also something more to ask. Apart from the slaughter tax, which is managed by the committee or recognized merchants, and the Management Office has full power to rectify, the remaining tooth tax and busy canal special funds are managed by the finance bureaus or magistrates of various counties, who can arbitrarily transfer funds. The Management Office has no power to remove them and has repeatedly urged them, but they disregard us. The misuse of busy canal funds, which are levied as an attachment, is even more serious. Previously, the 21st meeting of the esteemed committee resolved to ask the Education Department to consult with the Provincial Government and the Finance Department to order the finance bureaus of various counties that no matter what expenses are related to education funds, they are not allowed to be transferred, and the busy canal funds should be divided. With this proposal, we thought we could proceed accordingly, but the finance bureaus of various counties nominally divided the busy canal funds but still misused them. Despite the serious negotiations by the supervisors, many were still outwardly compliant but inwardly resistant and unwilling to earnestly implement the division and store the funds in banks. In such a situation, even the original education special funds will be greatly affected. We also hope that the esteemed committee will review the previous case and again ask the Provincial Government and the Finance Department to strictly order the finance bureaus of various counties to earnestly implement the division and separate storage of the busy canal funds and not transfer or default in any way. Any non-compliant officers should be dismissed and ordered to clear the funds and return them. This will be enough to demonstrate deterrence. We still hope for a reply. This is addressed to the Jiangsu Education Funding Committee.

Preparations for Celebrating Sun Yat-sen's Birthday at the Provincial Mass Education Center 122

The Jiangsu Provincial Mass Education Center, located in the Fan Gong Bridge in Zhenjiang City, believes that since the anniversary of Sun Yat-sen's birthday is imminent, the public should understand Sun Yat-sen's lifelong revolutionary history and fully understand the meaning of the Kuomintang. The center is organizing a campaign centered on this, with the promotion department in charge of preparations. The various pieces of news obtained by this newspaper are recorded as follows:

Compiling a Chronological Table of Sun Yat-sen's Life 123

In addition to posting slogans and printing leaflets, the promotion department is compiling a chronological table of Sun Yat-sen's life, printing delicate cards, and distributing them to the public. The content begins with Sun Yat-sen's birth on November 12th of the 5th year of the Tongzhi reign in Cuiheng Village, Xiangshan County, Guangdong Province, and describes his brief history year by year until his death on March 12th of the 14th year of the Republic of China. Everything is recorded in detail.

Forming Groups to Promote the History of the Revolution 124

In addition to participating in the parade organized by the Provincial Capital Propaganda Committee, the center is organizing two teams to give lectures in the experimental area and distant places. The themes are "Sun Yat-sen's Life" and "The History of the Revolution" and "The Meaning of the Party." It is heard that everything is being prepared and the work is about to begin.

The Exhibition Department Displays a Memorial Room 125

For the anniversary of Sun Yat-sen's birthday, the center is paying attention to activities outside the building. Inside the building, the exhibition department and the citizen's library are planning a memorial room. Photographs of Sun Yat-sen's life and his involvement in the revolutionary movement, as well as his lifelong works, are being collected and displayed in two rooms: (1) the Party Ideology Department of the Citizen Education Exhibition Room; (2) the Library Reading Room. It is currently being prepared and decorated. Anyone who wishes to commemorate Sun Yat-sen's great history and fully understand the meaning of the Kuomintang can go there for reference.

This Local Area 126

Minister of Education of Fujian Province, Cheng Shih-kuei, Returns to Shanghai 127

Recounts his ordeal

Cheng Shih-kuei, member of the Fujian Provincial Government and concurrently Minister of Education of the province, was detained in Youxi along with Lin Chih-yuan and others in January of this year for challenging Lu Hsing-pang over the province's education budget. Except for Chen Nai-yuan, who died, the other five provincial officials were fortunately spared. It was only recently that the reporter learned that Mr. Cheng and the others arrived in Shanghai the night before last. Yesterday afternoon, the reporter visited Mr. Cheng and learned the full details as follows: Soon after being detained, Mr. Cheng and the others were taken to the Youxi Command Headquarters, where the three officials lived together in a small room. All meals and daily life took place there. Normally, they were only allowed to read leisure books, and all newspapers were forbidden. All correspondence had to be collected and forwarded by Secretary Wang, but whether or not the contents were delivered depended entirely on the whims of the guards. During the detention, they were repeatedly on the verge of death, but the officials had long put their lives aside. Now, they were fortunate to regain their freedom, like a second life. After being released, they attended a welcome rally held by local people in Fujian, and then, together with Chairman Yang Shu-chuang, Lin Sen, Hsu Hsien-shih, Cheng Pao-ch'ing, and Wu Shu, they took the Yongjian warship to Shanghai. They arrived at Wusong at eleven o'clock the night before last and arrived here yesterday morning. Mr. Cheng is currently residing at No. 85 Jingxiu Road, Ximen. It is said that he intends to rest for a while before going to Nanjing to report everything. It is also said that Mr. Cheng wrote two volumes of diary during his detention, which may be printed into a booklet in the future to leave a trace.

Yu Yu-jen Resolves to Take Office as President of China National University

Expression to Tsai Yuan-pei and Students 128

(Kuomintang News Agency) The issue of the presidency of China National University in Wusong has attracted much attention in society. After the school board approved Ma Chun-wu's resignation and appointed Yu Yu-jen as his successor, most students were eager for Mr. Yu to take office as soon as possible. However, because Mr. Yu was slow to respond, the welcoming atmosphere seemed superficially quiet. A small number of students took the opportunity to campaign for Mr. Ma to return. At this time of transition, the school has fallen into a state of anarchy. It is now learned that Mr. Yu has decided to comply with the wishes of the school board and succeed as president. Recently, the student body has organized a student association to resolve the student unrest and issued a declaration requesting the school board to promptly implement the resolution and urge the successor to take charge of the school. Details are as follows:

Tsai Yuan-pei Urges Mr. Yu to Take Office On the third of this month, Tsai Yuan-pei personally went to urge Mr. Yu to take office as soon as possible. Mr. Yu said that he originally did not intend to interfere, but seeing the complex situation within the school in recent days, he would not decline the position. However, the date of taking office has not yet been determined.

Yu Yu-jen Expresses Responsibility On the evening of the fifth of this month, because the school was in a state of panic and urgently needed a new president to take office, the students separately sent eight representatives to visit Mr. Yu at his private residence to urge him to take office as soon as possible to appease the public and to inquire about the exact date of taking office so that a grand welcome ceremony could be held. Mr. Yu earnestly expressed to the representatives that he was a founder of China National University and, although he had been somewhat estranged from the school's situation, he had always been very concerned. This time, the school board asked him to be the president. He originally declined due to his declining strength, but the school board has already expressed its intentions and the situation within the school is becoming increasingly complex. If this delay continues, it would harm the school's future and the students' studies. He would take full responsibility for the party and the school to satisfy them. Mr. Ma would definitely not return to be the president. Currently, everything needs to be prepared, and there will be a satisfactory statement soon. It is late, and Wusong is far away. They can go back to school with peace of mind. He would not disappoint them. It is now heard that the students are actively preparing for a welcome ceremony, and it is said that Mr. Yu will take office before attending the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee.

Nine Organizations Hold Joint Meeting The student associations of China National University from Sichuan, Jiangxi, Anhui, Wujin, and the pre-second grade association, and other nine organizations held a joint meeting the day before yesterday afternoon and resolved the following important matters: (1) Organize the China National University Student Alliance to Resolve the Student Unrest; (2) Send representatives to visit Chairman Tsai to report on the actual situation within the school and expose the inside story of the illegal delegation; (3) Request the school board to promptly implement the resolution; (4) Issue a declaration to the outside world; (5) Issue a notice internally. It is also heard that the representatives sent by the joint association went to contact various parties yesterday.

Students Host Press The entire student delegation hosted reporters from major newspapers and news agencies in Shanghai at the Atlantic Hotel at 8 p.m. the day before yesterday (the 6th). First, Pang Mengfei, a representative of the delegation, detailed the remote causes and effects of the unrest, and then expressed that the will of more than a thousand students would not stop until the goal of retaining Ma was achieved.

Further News on the Student Unrest at Nanyang Medical College 129

The details of the student unrest at Nanyang Medical College in this city, which led to the expulsion of the president, have been reported in various newspapers. Yesterday, the school sealed off the classrooms and notified the professors to stop teaching. It is heard that the student union has hired a lawyer to publish a statement representing that it will resolve the matter according to law.

10th Japanese National Games 130

Only Three New Records Were Created Due to the Absence of First-Class Athletes

Masaru Hisatomi (Men's 800m), Tatsuo Saitsu (Decathlon)

Sadako Yamamoto (Women's 800m)

October 27, Osaka Dispatch The 17th National Games, organized by the Japan Association of Athletics Federations, was held at the Osaka Municipal Stadium on the 25th and 26th of this month. On the first day, due to the rain, the records of each event were not very special. On the second day, the weather finally recovered, and the athletes showed their skills and created three new records. One was Masaru Hisatomi's 800m, Tatsuo Saitsu's decathlon, and Sadako Yamamoto's women's 800m, all of which broke Japan's recognized records. Before the meeting, according to general predictions, at least seven or eight new records would be created this time. However, because Japan's first-class athletes did not participate, there was less excitement. For example, Kimura, who holds the high jump record, Nishida, who is second in the world in the pole vault, Oda, who won the world triple jump championship, Kudo, who runs the 10,000m, and Yoshioka and Nakajima, who run short distances, all announced their withdrawal because they wanted to give opportunities to newcomers. The audience on both days was very crowded. The records of men's and women's events, except for the 100m, were all very high. Compared with the results of our country's National Games, it is inevitable that they are far behind. The results of each event are recorded below:
